         b'e structural analysis and digital  reconstruction. Membrane-based se'

         b'egregation patterns are considered to be sorted into three types, fu'
         b'll cross\n(segregating 1:1:1:1), F2 cross (segregating 1:2:1), an'
         b'd test cross (segregating 1:1). The model selection criteria\nof '

         b'polynomial, but also to discriminate the QTL\nsegregation pattern'
         b'. 3FunMap can plot the log-likelihood ratio (LR) profiles along the '
         b'whole genome and the Legendre\npolynomial curves for each QTL gen'
         b'otype. In practical QTL mapping, the threshold of LR for each QTL mo'
         b'del can be\nobtained through permutations.\n\n\nFor more details, pl'

         b'iv id="bodyContent">\n\t\t\t\t<h1>3Dscript</h1>\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t'
         b'<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"'
         b'><table class="infobox" cellspacing="5" style="max-width: 31em; font'
         b'-size: 90%; text-align: left; float: right; border: 1px solid #a0a0a'
         b'0;">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="2" style="text-align: center; font'
         b'-size: 130%;"> <div style="float: left"></div>3Dscript (Fiji)<div st'
         b'yle="clear: left;"></div>\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<th> Author\n</th>\n'
         b'<td> <a href="/User:Bene" title="User:Bene">Benjamin Schmid</a>\n'
         b'</td></tr>\n\n\n\n\n<tr>\n<th> Maintainer\n</th>\n<td> <a href="/Use'
         b'r:Bene" title="User:Bene">Benjamin Schmid</a>\n</td></tr>\n\n\n<'
         b'tr>\n<th> Source\n</th>\n<td> <a rel="nofollow" class="external tex'
         b't" href="https://github.com/bene51/3Dscript/">on GitHub</a>\n</td'
         b'></tr>\n<tr>\n<th> Initial release\n</th>\n<td> January 2019\n</t'
         b'd></tr>\n\n<tr>\n<th> Development status\n</th>\n<td> active\n</td'
         b'></tr>\n<tr>\n<th> Category\n</th>\n<td> <a href="/Category:Visualiz'
         b'ation" title="Category:Visualization">Visualization</a>, <a href="/C'
         b'ategory:Plugins" title="Category:Plugins">Category:Plugins</a>\n<'
         b'/td></tr>\n\n</tbody></table>\n<p><br>\n</p>\n<div class="floatle'
         b'ft"><a href="/File:3Dscript-Logo.png" class="image"><img alt="3Dscri'
         b'pt-Logo.png" src="/_images/thumb/d/d9/3Dscript-Logo.png/160px-3Dscri'
         b'pt-Logo.png" width="160" height="160" srcset="/_images/thumb/d/d9/3D'
         b'script-Logo.png/240px-3Dscript-Logo.png 1.5x, /_images/thumb/d/d9/3D'
         b'script-Logo.png/320px-3Dscript-Logo.png 2x"></a></div>\n<p><b>3Ds'
         b'cript</b> - Create high-quality 3D/4D animations using a natural-lan'
         b'guage based syntax\n</p><p>In state-of-the-art 3D rendering and a'
         b'nimation software the user typically creates an animation by specify'
         b'ing a number of keyframes. While intuitive, this approach becomes te'
         b'dious for complex motions like simultaneous rotations around multipl'
         b'e axes, and even worse for accelerated and decelerated motions: The '
         b'number of required keyframes increases, and creating them becomes ha'
         b'rdly reproducible.\n</p><p>In 3Dscript, animations are defined by'
         b' a syntax based on natural English language, in sentences such as "F'
         b'rom frame 0 to frame 100 rotate by 360 degrees horizontally ease-in"'
         b'.\n</p><p><a href="/File:3Dscript-wiki-01.jpg" class="image"><img'
         b' alt="3Dscript-wiki-01.jpg" src="/_images/7/7e/3Dscript-wiki-01.jpg"'
         b' width="868" height="520"></a>\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><d'
         b'iv id="toctitle"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctoggle">&nbsp;[<a '
         b'role="button" tabindex="0" id="togglelink">hide</a>]&nbsp;</span></d'
         b'iv>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1"><a href="#Publicati'
         b'on"><span class="tocnumber">1</span> <span class="toctext">Publicati'
         b'on</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-2"><a href="'
         b'#Installation"><span class="tocnumber">2</span> <span class="toctext'
         b'">Installation</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-'
         b'3"><a href="#Quick_start"><span class="tocnumber">3</span> <span cla'
         b'ss="toctext">Quick start</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 t'
         b'ocsection-4"><a href="#User_documentation"><span class="tocnumber">4'
         b'</span> <span class="toctext">User documentation</span></a></li>'
         b'\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Publication">Pu'
         b'blication</span></h2>\n<ul><li> <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ve'
         b'r=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&am'
         b'p;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.title=3Dscript%3A+animating+3D%2F4D+microsc'
         b'opy+data+using+a+natural-language-based+syntax&amp;rft.aulast=Schmid'
         b'&amp;rft.aufirst=B.&amp;rft.date=2019&amp;rft.volume=16%284%29&amp;r'
         b'ft.pages=278%E2%80%93280&amp;rft_id=info:pmid/30886414&amp;rft_id=ht'
         b'tps%3A%2F%2Fwww.nature.com%2Farticles%2Fs41592-019-0359-1"><cite id='
         b'"CITEREFSchmidTripalFraa.C3.9FKersten2019">Schmid, B.; Tripal, P. &a'
         b'mp; Fraa\xc3\x9f, T. et al. (2019), "<a rel="nofollow" class="exte'
         b'rnal text" href="https://www.nature.com/articles/s41592-019-0359-1">'
         b'3Dscript: animating 3D/4D microscopy data using a natural-language-b'
         b'ased syntax</a>", <i>Nature methods</i> <b>16(4)</b>:  278\xe2\x80'
         b'\x93280, PMID 30886414<span class="printonly">, &lt;<a rel="nofollo'
         b'w" class="external free" href="https://www.nature.com/articles/s4159'
         b'2-019-0359-1">https://www.nature.com/articles/s41592-019-0359-1</a>&'
         b'gt;</span></cite></span>.</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline'
         b'" id="Installation">Installation</span></h2>\n<ul><li> Click on H'
         b'elp&gt;Update...</li>\n<li> Click on Manage update sites</li>\n<li'
         b"> Check the box in front of '3Dscript'</li>\n<li> Click on Close<"
         b'/li>\n<li> Click on Apply changes</li>\n<li> Restart Fiji</li></ul'
         b'>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Quick_start">Quick start</sp'
         b'an></h2>\n<ul><li> Click on File&gt;Open Samples&gt;T1 Head</li>\n'
         b'<li> Click on Plugins&gt;3D script&gt;Interactive Animation</li>'
         b'\n<li> In the "Interactive Raycaster" window, click on "show" nex'
         b't to "Animation"</li>\n<li> Click on "Start text-based animation '
         b'editor"</li>\n<li> In the editor window, type the following text:'
         b' From frame 0 to frame 200 rotate by 360 degrees horizontally</l'
         b'i>\n<li> Click on "Run" This will render 200 frames of a movie se'
         b'quence, within which the MRI data set rotates by 360 degrees.</li></'
         b'ul>\n<p><br>\nRendering of 200 frames of this data set will typica'
         b'lly take less than a minute on an OpenCL-enabled Graphics Card. The '
         b"resulting stack can be saved as a video file using Fiji's File&gt;Sa"
         b've As&gt;AVI... command.\n</p><p>To run the software on another d'
         b'ata set, open a different image stack (instead of the T1 Head sample'
         b' data) before running 3Dscript.\n</p><p>More information is avail'
         b'able at <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://bene51'
         b'.github.io/3Dscript">https://bene51.github.io/3Dscript</a>.\n</p>'
         b'\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="User_documentation">User docu'
         b'mentation</span></h2>\n<p>See 3Dscript in action below:\n</p><p><i'
         b'frame width="600" height="355" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/eR'
         b'rSoAubv6w" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen=""></iframe>  \n</p><p'
         b'><br>\nMore examples can be found on <a rel="nofollow" class="ext'
         b'ernal free" href="https://bene51.github.io/3Dscript/gallery.html">ht'
         b'tps://bene51.github.io/3Dscript/gallery.html</a>.\n</p><p>A full '
         b'manual as <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://bene'
         b'51.github.io/3Dscript/Manual.pdf">PDF</a>.\n</p>\n<!-- \nNewPP limi'

         b'\n        <div id="messagearea" class="empty">\n            \n     '
         b'       \n            \n            \n        </div>\n        <div cl'
         b'ass="rprt_all"><div class="rprt abstract"><div class="cit"><span rol'
         b'e="menubar"><a href="#" title="Bioinformatics (Oxford, England)." ab'
         b'stractlink="yes" alsec="jour" alterm="Bioinformatics." role="menuite'
         b'm" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="true">Bioinformatics.</a></s'
         b'pan> 2020 Mar 1;36(5):1367-1373. doi: 10.1093/bioinformatics/btz775.'
         b'</div><h1>Studying 3D genome evolution using genomic sequence.</h1><'
         b'div class="auths"><a href="/pubmed/?term=Mourad%20R%5BAuthor%5D&amp;'
         b'cauthor=true&amp;cauthor_uid=31605131">Mourad R</a><sup>1</sup>.</di'
         b'v><div class="afflist" style="zoom: 1;"><h3 style="zoom: 1;"><a titl'
         b'e="Open/close author information list" class="jig-ncbitoggler ui-wid'
         b'get ui-ncbitoggler" href="#" id="ui-ncbitoggler-2" role="button" ari'
         b'a-expanded="false"><span class="ui-ncbitoggler-master-text">Author i'
         b'nformation</span><span class="ui-icon ui-icon-triangle-1-e"></span><'
         b'/a></h3><div class="ui-helper-reset" aria-live="assertive"><dl class'
         b'="ui-ncbi-toggler-slave ui-ncbitoggler ui-ncbitoggler-slave" aria-hi'
         b'dden="true"><dt>1</dt><dd>LBCMCP, Centre de Biologie Int\xc3\xa9gr'
         b'ative (CBI), Universit\xc3\xa9 de Toulouse, CNRS, UPS, 31062 Toulo'
         b'use, France.</dd></dl></div></div><div class="abstr"><h3>Abstract</h'
         b'3><div class=""><h4>MOTIVATION: </h4><p>The three dimensions (3D) ge'
         b'nome is essential to numerous key processes such as the regulation o'
         b'f gene expression and the replication-timing program. In vertebrates'
         b', chromatin looping is often mediated by CTCF, and marked by CTCF mo'
         b'tif pairs in convergent orientation. Comparative high-throughput seq'
         b'uencing technique (Hi-C) recently revealed that chromatin looping ev'
         b'olves across species. However, Hi-C experiments are complex and cost'
         b'ly, which currently limits their use for evolutionary studies over a'
         b' large number of species.</p><h4>RESULTS: </h4><p>Here, we propose a'
         b' novel approach to study the 3D genome evolution in vertebrates usin'
         b'g the genomic sequence only, e.g. without the need for Hi-C data. Th'
         b'e approach is simple and relies on comparing the distances between c'
         b'onvergent and divergent CTCF motifs by computing a ratio we named th'
         b"e 3D ratio or '3DR'. We show that 3DR is a powerful statistic to det"
         b'ect CTCF looping encoded in the human genome sequence, thus reflecti'
         b'ng strong evolutionary constraints encoded in DNA and associated wit'
         b'h the 3D genome. When comparing vertebrate genomes, our results reve'
         b'al that 3DR which underlies CTCF looping and topologically associati'
         b'ng domain organization evolves over time and suggest that ancestral '
         b'character reconstruction can be used to infer 3DR in ancestral genom'
         b'es.</p><h4>AVAILABILITY AND IMPLEMENTATION: </h4><p>The R code is av'
         b'ailable at https://github.com/morphos30/PhyloCTCFLooping.</p><h4>SUP'
         b'PLEMENTARY INFORMATION: </h4><p>Supplementary data are available at '
         b'Bioinformatics online.</p><p class="copyright">\xc2\xa9 The Author'
         b'(s) 2019. Published by Oxford University Press. All rights reserved.'
         b' For permissions, please e-mail: journals.permissions@oup.com.</p></'
         b'div></div><div class="aux"><div class="resc"><dl class="rprtid"><dt>'
         b'PMID:</dt> <dd><span class="highlight" style="background-color:">316'
         b'05131</span></dd>  <dt>DOI:</dt> <dd><a href="//doi.org/10.1093/bioi'
         b'nformatics/btz775" ref="aid_type=doi" target="_blank">10.1093/bioinf'
         b'ormatics/btz775</a></dd> </dl></div><div class="resc status"></div><'

         b'\n\n\n<center>\n<img src="3DRobot.png" border="0">\n</center>\n<p>'
         b'</p><div align="justify">\n<br>\n\n3DRobot is a program devoted for'
         b' automated generation of diverse and well-packed protein \nstruct'
         b'ure decoys. Given a native structure as input, 3DRobot first identif'
         b'ies diverse \nstructure scaffolds from a non-redundant PDB librar'
         b'y. Restraint-free fragment reassembly \nsimulations are then perf'
         b'ormed to construct diverse full-length models.\nThe final decoys '
         b'are further refined at atomic-level by a two-step iterative ener'
         b'gy \nminimization procedure to improve the hydrogen-binding netwo'
         b'rks and steric overlaps of \nthe structures.\n3DRobot aims to prov'
         b'ide high-quality protein structural decoy sets for designing and'
         b' \ntraining protein folding force field and folding simulation me'
         b'thods \n(<a href="http://zhanglab.ccmb.med.umich.edu/3DRobot/abou'
         b't.html">&gt;&gt; More about the server ...</a>)\n<p>\n\n<!--<font c'
